304→func (c *objectCache) Get(namespace, name string) (runtime.Object, error) {\n   305→\tkey := objectKey{namespace: namespace, name: name}\n   306→\n   307→\tc.lock.RLock()\n   308→\titem, exists := c.items[key]\n   309→\tc.lock.RUnlock()\n   310→\n   311→\tif !exists {\n   312→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"object %q/%q not registered\", namespace, name)\n   313→\t}\n   314→\t// Record last access time independently if it succeeded or not.\n   315→\t// This protects from premature (racy) reflector closure.\n   316→\titem.setLastAccessTime(c.clock.Now())\n   317→\n   318→\t// Don't restart reflector if Kubelet is already shutting down.\n   319→\tif !c.isStopped() {\n   320→\t\titem.restartReflectorIfNeeded()\n   321→\t}\n   322→\tif err := wait.PollImmediate(10*time.Millisecond, time.Second, item.hasSynced); err != nil {\n   323→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to sync %s cache: %v\", c.groupResource.String(), err)\n   324→\t}\n   325→\tobj, exists, err := item.store.GetByKey(c.key(namespace, name))\n   326→\tif err != nil {\n   327→\t\treturn nil, err\n   328→\t}\n   329→\tif !exists {\n   330→\t\treturn nil, apierrors.NewNotFound(c.groupResource, name)\n   331→\t}\n   332→\tif object, ok := obj.(runtime.Object); ok {\n   333→\t\t// If the returned object is immutable, stop the reflector.\n   334→\t\t//\n   335→\t\t// NOTE: we may potentially not even start the reflector if the object is\n   336→\t\t// already immutable. However, given that:\n   337→\t\t// - we want to also handle the case when object is marked as immutable later\n   338→\t\t// - Secrets and ConfigMaps are periodically fetched by volumemanager anyway\n   339→\t\t// - doing that wouldn't provide visible scalability/performance gain - we\n   340→\t\t//   already have it from here\n   341→\t\t// - doing that would require significant refactoring to reflector\n   342→\t\t// we limit ourselves to just quickly stop the reflector here.\n   343→\t\tif c.isImmutable(object) {\n   344→\t\t\titem.setImmutable()\n   345→\t\t\tif item.stop() {\n   346→\t\t\t\tklog.V(4).InfoS(\"Stopped watching for changes - object is immutable\", \"obj\", klog.KRef(namespace, name))\n   347→\t\t\t}\n   348→\t\t}\n   349→\t\treturn object, nil\n   350→\t}\n   351→\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected object type: %v\", obj)\n   352→}\n   353→\n   354→func (c *objectCache) startRecycleIdleWatch() {\n   355→\tc.lock.Lock()\n   356→\tdefer c.lock.Unlock()\n   357→\n   358→\tfor key, item := range c.items {\n   359→\t\tif item.stopIfIdle(c.clock.Now(), c.maxIdleTime) {\n   360→\t\t\tklog.V(4).InfoS(\"Not acquired for long time, Stopped watching for changes\", \"objectKey\", key, \"maxIdleTime\", c.maxIdleTime)\n   361→\t\t}\n   362→\t}\n   363→}\n   364→\n   365→func (c *objectCache) shutdownWhenStopped(stopCh <-chan struct{}) {\n   366→\t<-stopCh\n   367→\n   368→\tc.lock.Lock()\n   369→\tdefer c.lock.Unlock()\n   370→\n   371→\tc.stopped = true\n   372→\tfor _, item := range c.items {\n   373→\t\titem.stop()\n   374→\t}\n   375→}\n   376→\n   377→// NewWatchBasedManager creates a manager that keeps a cache of all objects\n   378→// necessary for registered pods.\n   379→// It implements the following logic:\n   380→//   - whenever a pod is created or updated, we start individual watches for all\n   381→//     referenced objects that aren't referenced from other registered pods\n   382→//   - every GetObject() returns a value from local cache propagated via watches\n   383→func NewWatchBasedManager(\n   384→\tlistObject listObjectFunc,\n   385→\twatchObject watchObjectFunc,\n   386→\tnewObject newObjectFunc,\n   387→\tisImmutable isImmutableFunc,\n   388→\tgroupResource schema.GroupResource,\n   389→\tresyncInterval time.Duration,\n   390→\tgetReferencedObjects func(*v1.Pod) sets.Set[string]) Manager {\n   391→\n   392→\t// If a configmap/secret is used as a volume, the volumeManager will visit the objectCacheItem every resyncInterval cycle,\n   393→\t// We just want to stop the objectCacheItem referenced by environment variables,\n   394→\t// So, maxIdleTime is set to an integer multiple of resyncInterval,\n   395→\t// We currently set it to 5 times.\n   396→\tmaxIdleTime := resyncInterval * 5\n   397→\n   398→\t// TODO propagate stopCh from the higher level.\n   399→\tobjectStore := NewObjectCache(listObject, watchObject, newObject, isImmutable, groupResource, clock.RealClock{}, maxIdleTime, wait.NeverStop)\n   400→\treturn NewCacheBasedManager(objectStore, getReferencedObjects)\n   401→}\n   402→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. {\n\t\t\tdelete(item.refMap, referencedFrom)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif len(item.refMap) == 0 {\n\t\t\t// Stop the underlying reflector.\n\t\t\titem.stop()\n\t\t\tdelete(c.items, key)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// key returns key of an object with a given name and namespace.\n// This has to be in-sync with cache.MetaNamespaceKeyFunc.\nfunc (c *objectCache) key(namespace, name string) string {\n\tif len(namespace) > 0 {\n\t\treturn namespace + \"/\" + name\n\t}\n\treturn name\n}\n\nfunc (c *objectCache) isStopped() bool {\n\tc.lock.RLock()\n\tdefer c.lock.RUnlock()\n\treturn c.stopped\n}\n\nfunc (c *objectCache) Get(namespace, name string) (runtime.Object, error) {\n\tkey := objectKey{namespace: namespace, name: name}\n\n\tc.lock.RLock()\n\titem, exists := c.items[key]\n\tc.lock.RUnlock()\n\n\tif !exists {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"object %q/%q not registered\", namespace, name)\n\t}\n\t// Record last access time independently if it succeeded or not.\n\t// This protects from premature (racy) reflector closure.\n\titem.setLastAccessTime(c.clock.Now())\n\n\t// Don't restart reflector if Kubelet is already shutting down.\n\tif !c.isStopped() {\n\t\titem.restartReflectorIfNeeded()\n\t}\n\tif err := wait.PollImmediate(10*time.Millisecond, time.Second, item.hasSynced); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to sync %s cache: %v\", c.groupResource.String(), err)\n\t}\n\tobj, exists, err := item.store.GetByKey(c.key(namespace, name))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tif !exists {\n\t\treturn nil, apierrors.NewNotFound(c.groupResource, name)\n\t}\n\tif object, immutable. However, given that:\n\t\t// - we want to also handle the case when object is marked as immutable later\n\t\t// - Secrets and ConfigMaps are periodically fetched by volumemanager anyway\n\t\t// - doing that wouldn't provide visible scalability/performance gain - we\n\t\t//   already have it from here\n\t\t// - doing that would require significant refactoring to reflector\n\t\t// we limit ourselves to just quickly stop the reflector here.\n\t\tif c.isImmutable(object) {\n\t\t\titem.setImmutable()\n\t\t\tif item.stop() {\n\t\t\t\tklog.V(4).InfoS(\"Stopped watching for changes - object is immutable\", \"obj\", klog.KRef(namespace, name))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn object, nil\n\t}\n\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected object type: %v\", obj)\n}\n\nfunc (c *objectCache) startRecycleIdleWatch() {\n\tc.lock.Lock()\n\tdefer c.lock.Unlock()\n\n\tfor key, item := range c.items {\n\t\tif item.stopIfIdle(c.clock.Now(), c.maxIdleTime) {\n\t\t\tklog.V(4).InfoS(\"Not acquired for long time, Stopped watching for changes\", \"objectKey\", key, \"maxIdleTime\", c.maxIdleTime)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (c *objectCache) shutdownWhenStopped(stopCh <-chan struct{}) {\n\t<-stopCh\n\n\tc.lock.Lock()\n\tdefer c.lock.Unlock()\n\n\tc.stopped = true\n\tfor _, item := range c.items {\n\t\titem.stop()\n\t}\n}\n\n// NewWatchBasedManager creates a manager that keeps a cache of all objects\n// necessary for registered pods.\n// It implements the following logic:\n//   - whenever a pod is created or updated, we start individual watches for all\n//     referenced objects that aren't referenced from other registered pods\n//   - every GetObject() returns a value from local cache propagated via watches\nfunc NewWatchBasedManager(\n\tlistObject listObjectFunc,\n\twatchObject watchObjectFunc,\n\tnewObject newObjectFunc,\n\tisImmutable isImmutableFunc,\n\tgroupResource schema.GroupResource,\n\tresyncInterval time.Duration,\n\tgetReferencedObjects func(*v1.Pod) sets.Set[string]) Manager {\n\n\t// If a configmap/secret is used as a volume, the volumeManager will visit the objectCacheItem every resyncInterval cycle,\n\t// We just want to stop the objectCacheItem referenced by environment variables,\n\t// So, maxIdleTime is set to an integer multiple of resyncInterval,\n\t// We currently set it to 5 times.\n\tmaxIdleTime := resyncInterval * 5\n\n\t// TODO propagate stopCh from the higher level.\n\tobjectStore := NewObjectCache(listObject, watchObject, newObject, isImmutable, groupResource, clock.RealClock{}, maxIdleTime, wait.NeverStop)\n\treturn NewCacheBasedManager(objectStore, getReferencedObjects)\n}\n","numLines":402,"startLine":1,"totalLines":402}}}

(staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go) for both ConfigMap and Secret objects. This field is a boolean pointer that, when set to true, prevents modification of the object's data.\\n\\n2. **Immutable Field Validation and Mutation Prevention**: The validation logic is implemented in pkg/apis/core/validation/validation.go with functions ValidateConfigMapUpdate() and ValidateSecretUpdate(). These functions prevent users from:\\n   - Unsetting the Immutable field once it's set to true\\n   - Modifying the Data field (for Secrets) or Data/BinaryData fields (for ConfigMaps) when Immutable is true\\n   The validation is called from the strategy patterns in pkg/registry/core/configmap/strategy.go and pkg/registry/core/secret/strategy.go through their ValidateUpdate() methods.\\n\\n3. **Watch Optimization**: The feature includes optimization in the kubelet to skip watching immutable objects for changes. This is implemented in:\\n   - pkg/kubelet/util/manager/watch_based_manager.go: The core watch-based manager that detects immutable objects when they are retrieved and stops the reflector/watcher for them (lines 333-348 in the Get() method). The objectCacheItem tracks immutability status and prevents restart of stopped reflectors if the object is immutable.\\n   - pkg/kubelet/configmap/configmap_manager.go: NewWatchingConfigMapManager() creates an isImmutable closure (lines 148-153) that checks if a ConfigMap has Immutable set to true.\\n   - pkg/kubelet/secret/secret_manager.go: NewWatchingSecretManager() creates an isImmutable closure (lines 149-154) that checks if a Secret has Immutable set to true.\\n   When the kubelet's volume manager retrieves an immutable ConfigMap or Secret, the watch-based manager automatically stops the watch since the object will never change, improving performance and reducing load on the apiserver.\\n\\nThe implementation ensures data consistency and cluster performance by preventing unauthorized mutations of immutable objects and reducing unnecessary watch operations for objects that will not change.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
